msg:In my impression, Crown Hotel is characterized by dense guest rooms, and its occupancy rate has always been high, but I always feel that it is in an awkward position among IHG. During this trip to Nanjing, I finally chose Crowne Plaza Nanjing Yincheng among several hotels because its price was not too abstract during the Spring Festival.

Then I was lucky enough to meet Miss Fanny Huang Shengnan, a very good staff member. I spontaneously wrote this to express my gratitude. Since the number of rooms was very tight during the Spring Festival, I didn't get the room type I wanted to book, so I scraped together room types for a few days. I felt sick just looking at them, and I thought it would be a long time to change rooms. Fanny understood the needs of our group and did her best to arrange a suitable room type and location for us. Although I did not book with my ihg membership number, she was very thoughtful and helped us upgrade. The room type is still very spacious, about 42 square meters. Although many people complain that the hotel facilities are old and to be honest, it is a bit "old", but it can be seen that the quality of the objects is not bad and the maintenance is also very good. Especially for a hotel that is not too new, the idea of ‚Äã‚Äãsetting up a separate toilet room to separate wet and dry toilets during the original design was quite advanced. The hotel's floor aunts are also warm and friendly. During the Chinese New Year, they have a heavy workload, but they can still greet us politely and provide us with the extra items we need. We must give them a thumbs up.

During our stay, there were several guests with children living nearby. Since the adults did not discipline them, these children ran around in the corridors, making noise, or visited each other and frequently closed and slammed the doors, which caused a lot of damage to our stay. Influence. I had no choice but to contact Fanny again and expressed that I was willing to pay more to ask her to change rooms for us. Unexpectedly, Fanny changed us to two rooms for free on Valentine's Day when the rooms were tight. Moreover, this time the room had a better view and surroundings. It has become much quieter. I am really grateful to Fanny for providing us with such high-quality services based on customer-centeredness and the vital interests of customers. Below the window is the best viewing area of ‚Äã‚ÄãBaijia Lake. Across the lake is Jingfeng's area. During the day, you can already enjoy the beautiful scenery of the manor of the lakeside Jinling Hotel downstairs. At night, the Ferris wheel on the lakeside and the collective lights of the surrounding buildings The lights, as well as the lights of the Lakeside Jinling Hotel downstairs, complement each other beautifully. You can also see beautiful fireworks on the fourth day of the ***** New Year. It is a wonderful night. Thank you Fanny for making our New Year trip come to a successful conclusion. Since we took the train at around three in the afternoon, Fanny also arranged a late check-out for us in advance. The outdoor temperature of the Big Blue Whale has been quite high these days. Thank you for allowing me to avoid secondary physical exertion after hiking at the Red Mountain Zoo. .

In addition, the location of the hotel is very convenient. Although it is located in Jiangning District, it is only 3 subway stops away from Nanjing South Railway Station. Shengtai Road Subway Station is nearby. Line 1 can go directly to Xinjiekou (not far from Kexiang). ), Drum Tower, Xuanwu Gate, Zhujiang Road, New Model Road, Hongshan Zoo, Nanjing Railway Station, South Railway Station and other landmark sites. It is also surrounded by Tongxi Business District and Baijiahu Business District (Jingfeng, Golden Eagle, etc.), as well as some well-known local restaurants such as Little Chef Huaiyang Cuisine, Geweixuan, Mingfeng Fish House, etc.

I didn't eat the breakfast, so I can't comment on it, but I read many reviews that their breakfast is a major feature, and I think that should be the case.

I also saw some comments about some problems with the hotel. Judging from the service I experienced during my stay, I feel that the hotel is actively improving and listening to customer opinions. After all, there are too many Blue Whale hotels, and Crown does not have an advantage in terms of hardware, but they strive to be the best in terms of improving services.
